False)\n    POP_JUMP_BACKWARD_IF_FALSE = generic_jump(operator.not_, False)\n\n    def CACHE(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        pass\n\n    def BEFORE_WITH(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        self.setup_or_before_with(inst)\n\n    def setup_or_before_with(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        ctx = self.pop()\n        if not isinstance(\n            ctx, (ContextWrappingVariable, GenericContextWrappingVariable)\n        ):\n            unimplemented_v2(\n                gb_type=\"Unsupported context manager\",\n                context=f\"Attempted SETUP_WITH/BEFORE_WITH on {ctx}\",\n                explanation=f\"Dynamo does not know how to enter a `{ctx.python_type_name()}` context manager.\",\n                hints=[\n                    \"Avoid using the unsupported context manager.\",\n                    \"If the context manager seems like it should be supported (e.g. torch.set_grad_enabled), then \"\n                    \"it may be the case that it was created outside the compiled region, which Dynamo does not support. \"\n                    \"Supported context managers can cross graph break boundaries only if they are local non-closure \"\n                    \"variables, or are intermediate values.\",\n                    \"File an issue to PyTorch. Simple context managers can potentially be supported, \"\n                    \"but note that context managers can't be supported in general\",\n                ],\n            )\n\n        if (\n            isinstance(ctx, GenericContextWrappingVariable)\n            and not ctx.supports_graph_breaks()\n        ):\n            self.active_generic_context_managers.append(ctx)\n\n        # Need this redundant check for mypy\n        assert isinstance(\n            ctx, (ContextWrappingVariable, GenericContextWrappingVariable)\n        )\n\n        exit = WithExitFunctionVariable(\n            ctx,\n            inst.target,\n        )\n\n        if sys.version_info >= (3, 11):\n            # See create_call_resume_at for block stack details.\n            # Only push a block if the current instruction's block is a\n            # with block that is not nested in a try block - that is, the current\n            # instruction's block target is the same as the top block's target.\n            if inst.exn_tab_entry and (\n                not self.block_stack\n                or inst.exn_tab_entry.target is not self.block_stack[-1].target\n            ):\n                target = None\n            else:\n                assert self.next_instruction.exn_tab_entry is not None\n                target = self.next_instruction.exn_tab_entry.target\n        else:\n            target = inst.target\n\n        self.push(exit)\n\n        if target:\n            if isinstance(self, InstructionTranslator) or config.nested_graph_breaks:\n                self.block_stack.append(\n                    BlockStackEntry(inst, target, len(self.stack), ctx)\n                )\n            else:\n                self.block_stack.append(BlockStackEntry(inst, target, len(self.stack)))\n\n        self.push(ctx.enter(self))\n\n    def append_prefix_inst(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        assert self.accept_prefix_inst\n        self.prefix_insts.append(inst)\n\n    def MAKE_CELL(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        if sys.version_info >= (3, 12) and not self.accept_prefix_inst:\n            # In 3.12+, MAKE_CELL is not longer necessarily a prefix instruction.\n            # self.output.side_effects.track_cell_new()\n            )\n        else:\n            self.append_prefix_inst(inst)\n\n    def COPY_FREE_VARS(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n down into\n    # BUILD_SLICE 2 and BINARY/STORE_SUBSCR\n\n    def END_FOR(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        if sys.version_info >= (3, 13):\n            self.pop()\n        else:\n      hints=[*graph_break_hints.USER_ERROR],\n            )\n        self.LOAD_FAST(inst)\n\n    def LOAD_FAST_AND_CLEAR(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        if inst.argval not in SET_FUNCTION_ATTRIBUTE(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n        flags = inst.arg\n        assert flags is not None\n        fn = self.pop()\n        assert isinstance(fn, NestedUserFunctionVariable)\n        attr = self.pop()\n\n        if flags & 0x08:\n            fn.closure = attr\n        elif flags & 0x04:\n            fn.annotations = attr\n        elif flags & 0x02:\n            fn.kwdefaults = attr\n        elif flags & 0x01:\n            fn.defaults = attr\n\n        self.push(fn)\n\n    def CONVERT_VALUE(self, inst: Instruction) -> None:\n     )\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        output: OutputGraph,\n        instructions: list[Instruction],\n        f_locals: dict[str, Any],\n        f_globals: dict[str, Any],\n        f_builtins: dict[str, Any],\n        code_options: dict[str, Any],\n        symbolic_locals: dict[str, VariableTracker],\n        symbolic_globals: dict[str, VariableTracker],\n    self.symbolic_locals = {}\n            # Populate `symbolic_locals` with non-cell variables.\n            cell_and_freevars: set[str] = set(self.cell_and_freevars())\n\n            dynamism = code_context.get_context(f_code).get(\"dynamism\", None)\n            for name, value in f_locals.items():\n                if name not in cell_and_freevars:\n                    local_dynamism = None\n                    if dynamism:\n                        local_dynamism = frozenset(dynamism.get(name, {}).items())\n                    var = LazyVariableTracker.create(\n                        value,\n                        LocalSource(\n                            name,\n                            is_input=True,\n                            dynamism=local_dynamism,\n                        ),\n                    )\n                    self.symbolic_locals[name] = var\n\n            # Populate `symbolic_locals` with cells created by this frame,\n            # effectively This models cells that are also function inputs.\n                    value = f_locals[name]\n                    # NOTE: root frame inputs that are captured by a nested\n                    # function become special cell objects -- they exist in\n                    # `f_locals` as contents of the cells, rather than the cells\n                    # objects themselves.\n                    #\n                    # In Dynamo, we choose to represent such input cell objects\n                    # as newly created (rather than pre-existing) cell objects,\n                    # because\n                    #\n                    # 1. The reason for representing a pre-existing cell object\n                    # is to emit guard or codegen mutations. However, local\n                    # cells should never be used for guards. Moreover, at this\n                    # point these input cell objects should've never been\n                    # accessed by anyone else, since Dynamo intercepts the frame\n                    # right after its evaluation starts, i.e., right after these\n                    # cell objects are created. So they should have no external\n                    # reference, meaning no mutation needs to be propagated.\n                    #\n                    # 2. This conveniently allows codegen to prune away\n                    # mutations to these cells, unless they escape the frame.\n                    contents_source = LocalSource(\n                        name, is_input=True, is_derefed_cell_contents=True\n                    )\n                    contents_var: VariableTracker = LazyVariableTracker.create(\n                        value,              cell_var = side_effects.track_cell_new()\n                cell_var.local_name = name  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n                self.symbolic_locals[name] = cell_var\n\n            # self.symbolic_locals\n                )\n\n    def _throw_if_in_functorch(self) -> None:\n        # Fallback to eager in case of a graph break inside vmap\n        eager = torch._C._functorch.TransformType.Jvp,\n        )\n\n        if ci is not None and ci.key() in forbidden_keys and compiler_fn is not eager:\n            name = ci.key().name.lower()\n            msg =          explanation=msg,\n                hints=[],\n            )\n\n    def get_example_value(self, source: Source) -> Any:\n        if isinstance(source, LocalSource):\n            return \"ir_count\", self.instruction_pointer - self.start_point\n        )\n\n        if (\n            not config.allow_empty_graphs\n            and self.output.count_calls() == 0\n            and not Any, kwargs: Any) -> Any:\n        with patch.dict(counters, {\"unimplemented\": counters[\"inline_call\"]}):\n            tracer = cls.build_inline_tracer(parent, func, args, kwargs)\n gb_type=\"Inline attempt with __self__\",\n                context=str(func),\n                explanation=\"Attempted to inline a function with the `__self__` attribute. \"\n                \"Dynamo is expected to decompose method calls into function calls with a `self` argument.\",\n                hints=[],\n            )\n\n        if isinstance(func, UserFunctionVariable) and inspect.getattr_static(\n            func.get_function(), \"_torchdynamo_disable\", False\n        ):\n            msg = inspect.getattr_static(\n                func.get_function(), \"_torchdynamo_disable_msg\", None\n            )\n            unimplemented_v2(\n                gb_type=\"Skip inlining `torch.compiler.disable()`d function\",\n                context=str(func.get_function()),\n                explanation=f\"Skip inlining function {func.get_function()} since it was wrapped \"\n                f\"with `torch.compiler.disable` (reason: {msg})\",\n                hints=[\n                    \"Remove the `torch.compiler.disable` call\",\n                ],\n            )\n\n        result = trace_rules.check_verbose(func, is_inlined_call=True)\n        if result.skipped:\n            from torch._dynamo.variables.misc import produce_trampoline_autograd_apply\n\n            # _origin marks this as coming from an internal dynamo known function that is safe to\n            # trace through.\n            if hasattr(getattr(func, \"fn\", None), \"_origin\") and func.fn._origin in [\n                produce_trampoline_autograd_apply,\n            ]:\n                # Known sound\n                return trace_rules.SkipResult(\n                    False, \"allowlist in dynamo known function\"\n                )\n            fn_qualname = func.fn.__qualname__ if hasattr(func, \"fn\") else \"\"\n            hints = [\n                f\"Avoid calling the function `{fn_qualname}`.\",\n            ]\n            if \"_dynamo\" not in func.get_filename():\n                hints += [\n                    f\"Apply `@torch._dynamo.dont_skip_tracing` to the function `{fn_qualname}` \"\n                    \"to force tracing into the function. \"\n                    \"More graph breaks may occur as a result of attempting to trace into the function.\",\n                    \"Please file an issue to PyTorch.\",\n                ]\n            unimplemented_v2(\n                gb_type=\"Attempted to inline function marked as skipped\",\n                context=f\"qualname: {fn_qualname}, name: function `{fn_qualname}` \"\n                \"should not be traced.\",\n                hints=hints,\n            )\n\n        return result\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def build_inline_tracer(\n        parent: Any,\n        func: VariableTracker,\n        args: list[VariableTracker],\n        kwargs: Any,\n    ) -> InliningInstructionTranslator:\n        assert isinstance(\n            func,\n            (\n                UserFunctionVariable,\n                NestedUserFunctionVariable,\n                LocalGeneratorFunctionVariable,\n                LocalGeneratorObjectVariable,\n            ),\n        )\n        code: types.CodeType = func.get_code()\n        result = None\n        tracing_ctx = parent.output.tracing_context\n\n        # Check if we have already identified this function to be inline-able.\n        # The exception is dont_skip_tracing flag which affects the inline\n        # behavior. If the flag is True, don't rely on previous results.\n        if not config.dont_skip_tracing and tracing_ctx:\n            if previous_result := tracing_ctx.previously_inlined_functions.get(\n                code, None\n            ):\n                result = previous_result\n\n        if result is None:\n            if isinstance(func, SkipFunctionVariable):\n                unimplemented_v2(\n                    gb_type=\"Attempted to inline function marked as skipped (SkipFunctionVariable)\",\n                    context=f\"Attempted to inline a SkipFunctionVariable {func}\",\n                    explanation=(\n                        \"Attempted to inline a function that was previously determined to be marked as intentionally skipped.\"\n                    ),\n                    hints=[],\n                )\n            result = InliningInstructionTranslator.check_inlineable(func)\n            assert result.skipped is False\n\n            if not config.dont_skip_tracing and tracing_ctx:\n                tracing_ctx.previously_inlined_functions[code] = result\n\n        try:\n            sub_locals = func.bind_args(parent, args, kwargs)\n        except TypeError as e:\n            # Wrap the general TypeError during bind_args() to the internal ArgsMismatchError with detailed info\n            raise ArgsMismatchError(  # noqa: B904\n                \"{reason}.\\n  func = {func}, args = {args}, kwargs = {kwargs}\".format(\n                    reason=str(e),\n                    func=f\"'{func.get_name()}' {func.get_filename()}:{func.get_code().co_firstlineno}\",\n                    args=[arg.python_type() for arg in args],\n                    kwargs=kwargs,\n                ),\n            )\n\n        for v in itertools.chain(sub_locals.values()):\n            if not isinstance(v, VariableTracker):\n                unimplemented_v2(\n                    gb_type=\"Encountered unconverted argument when attempting to inline\",\n                    context=f\"func: {func}, arg: {v}\",\n                    explanation=\"An argument to an inlined function was not successfully converted to a VariableTracker.\",\n                    hints=[*graph_break_hints.DYNAMO_BUG],\n                )\n\n        if code.co_name in (\"__setitem__\", \"__setattr__\") and not (\n            args and isinstance(args[0], variables.UserDefinedObjectVariable)\n        ):\n            unimplemented_v2(\n                gb_type=\"Unsupported __setitem__/__setattr__ inline attempt\",\n                context=f\"code name: {code.co_name}, args: {args}\",\n                explanation=f\"Attempted to inline {code.co_name} where first argument (self) is not a user-defined object.\",\n                hints=[],\n            )\n\n        suffix = \"\"\n        # TODO: mlazos, add support for enabling multiple artifact logs\n        # with a single alias\n        if torch._logging._internal.log_state.is_artifact_enabled(\"bytecode\"):\n            suffix = f\"\\n{dis.Bytecode(code).dis()}\"\n        if sys.version_info >= (3, 11):\n            cur_inst = parent.current_instruction\n            parent_code = parent.f_code\n\n            def get_trace_call_log_str() -> str:\n                header = parent.get_line_of_code_header(\n                    lineno=cur_inst.positions.lineno\n                )\n                line = get_instruction_source_311(parent_code, cur_inst).rstrip()\n                return f\"TRACE inlined call {code.co_name} from {header}\\n{line}\"\n\n            trace_call_log.debug(\"%s\", LazyString(get_trace_call_log_str))\n        log.debug(\"INLINING %s%s, %s\", code, suffix, result.reason)\n\n        # Detect inline GraphModule calls in order to propagate node metadata,\n        # by checking if the first argument (self) is a variable tracking a GraphModule.\n        if args and isinstance(args[0], NNModuleVariable):\n            module = parent.output.get_submodule(args[0].module_key)\n            if isinstance(module, torch.fx.GraphModule):\n                # The inline call might not actually be a call to `forward`,\n                # but it is enough to add a context for `forward` in case it is called.\n                code_context.get_context(module.forward.__code__)[\n                    \"orig_graphmodule\"\n                ] = weakref.ref(module)\n\n        tracer: InliningInstructionTranslator\n        if is_generator(code):\n            tracer = InliningGeneratorInstructionTranslator(\n                parent,\n                code,\n                sub_locals,\n                parent.symbolic_globals,\n                parent.symbolic_torch_function_state,\n                func,\n            )\n        else:\n            # need the line below to make MyPy happy\n            assert not isinstance(func, LocalGeneratorObjectVariable)\n            tracer = InliningInstructionTranslator(\n                parent,\n                code,\n                sub_locals,\n                parent.symbolic_globals,\n                parent.symbolic_torch_function_state,\n                func,\n            )\n        return tracer\n\n    def inline_call_(self) -> VariableTracker:\n        parent = self.parent\n        code = self.f_code\n\n        strict_ctx: Any = contextlib.nullcontext()\n        if parent.strict_checks_fn:\n            strict_ctx = self.strict_translation_mode(parent.strict_checks_fn)\n        try:\n            with strict_ctx:\n                self.run()\n        except exc.ObservedException as e:\n            msg = f\"Observed exception DURING INLING {code} : {e}\"\n            log.debug(msg)\n            # bubble up the exception to the parent frame.\n            raise\n        except exc.SkipFrame as e:\n            msg = f\"SKIPPED INLINING {code}: {e}\"\n            log.debug(msg)\n            raise Unsupported(msg) from e\n        except Exception:\n            log.debug(\"FAILED INLINING %s\", code)\n            raise\n        finally:\n            parent.error_on_graph_break = self.error_on_graph_break\n\n        if self.output.should_exit:\n            # graph break\n            return ConstantVariable.create(None)  # return dummy variable\n\n        assert self.symbolic_result is not None\n\n        if self.f_globals is parent.f_globals:\n            # Merge symbolic_globals back if parent and child are in the same namespace\n            parent.symbolic_globals.update(self.symbolic_globals)\n\n        parent.inconsistent_side_effects |= self.inconsistent_side_effects\n\n        log.debug(\"DONE INLINING %s\", code)\n        self.output.tracing_context.traced_code.append(code)\n\n        if config.enable_faithful_generator_behavior or (\n            isinstance(self, InliningGeneratorInstructionTranslator)\n            and self.is_generator_from_ctx_manager\n        ):\n            if (\n                is_generator(code)\n                and isinstance(self, InliningGeneratorInstructionTranslator)\n                and self.generator_exhausted\n            ):\n                assert isinstance(self, InliningGeneratorInstructionTranslator)\n                # When the generator returns None, we raise StopIteration\n                args = []\n                if not (\n                    isinstance(self.symbolic_result, ConstantVariable)\n                    and self.symbolic_result.value is None\n                ):\n                    args = [self.symbolic_result]\n                exc.raise_observed_exception(StopIteration, self, args=args)\n            else:\n                return self.symbolic_result\n        else:\n            if is_generator(code):\n                assert isinstance(self, InliningGeneratorInstructionTranslator)\n                assert self.symbolic_result.as_python_constant() is None\n                return ListIteratorVariable(\n                    self.generated_items,\n                    mutation_type=ValueMutationNew(),\n                )\n            else:\n                return self.symbolic_result\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        parent: InstructionTranslatorBase,\n        code: types.CodeType,\n        symbolic_locals: dict[str, VariableTracker],\n        symbolic_globals: dict[str, VariableTracker],\n        symbolic_torch_function_state: SymbolicTorchFunctionState,\n        funcvar: BaseUserFunctionVariable,\n    ) -> None:\n        f_globals = funcvar.get_globals()  #         instructions = tracing_ctx.previously_cleaned_instructions[code]\n\n        if instructions is None:\n            instructions = cleaned_instructions(code)\n symbolic_globals=symbolic_globals,\n            symbolic_torch_function_state=symbolic_torch_function_state,\n            instructions=instructions,\n            code_options={k: getattr(code, k) for @property\n    def fake_mode(self) -> Optional[FakeTensorMode]:\n        return self.parent.fake_mode\n\n    def run_ctx_mgr(self) -> Any:\n        return ReturnValueOp\n\n    def get_globals_source_and_value(\n        self, name: str\n    ) -> tuple[Any, VariableTracker, Source]:\n        # NamedTuple's `__new__` has a fake global scope that's not an TODO generalize the check for other non-importable cases.\n        # https://github.com/python/cpython/blob/8421b03b16a4852a527256cb7cdce2ab2d318548/Lib/collections/__init__.py#L441-L447\n        if \"__name__\" in self.f_globals and not self.f_globals[\"__name__\"].startswith(\n            \"namedtuple_\"\n        ):\n            module_name = self.f_globals[\"__name__\"]\n            module_source = self.import_source(module_name)\n            if \"torch_package\" in module_name:\n                fglobals_value = (\n                    torch.package.package_importer._package_imported_modules[\n                        module_name\n                    ]\n                )  # torch._dynamo.graph_break()\n                return torch.mm(x, y) + self.bias\n\n            def forward(self, x):\n                a_float32 = torch.rand((8, 8), device=\"cpu\")\n          return orig_func(*args, **kwargs)\n\n            return new_fwd\n\n        def autocast_func_cuda(orig_func):\n            @torch.autocast(device_type=\"cuda\", dtype=torch.float16)\n            def new_fwd(*args, **kwargs):\n                return orig_func(*args, **kwargs)\n\n            return new_fwd\n\n        def autocast_func_cpu(orig_func):\n          torch._dynamo.reset()\n\n                ctx_wrapper, _ = ctx_wrappers[i]\n                ctx_wrapper_inverse, mode_inverse = ctx_wrappers[(i + 1) % 2]\n\n                def fn(x):\n Based on an example from omegaconfig.listconfig\n    class ListIterator(Iterator[Any]):\n        def __init__(self, lst: Any, resolve: bool) -> None:\n            self.resolve = resolve\n            self.iterator = iter(lst.__dict__[\"_content\"])\n            self.index = 0\n\n        def __next__(self) -> Any:\n            x = next(self.iterator)\n            if self.resolve:\n                x = x._dereference_node()\n                if x._is_missing():\n                    raise AssertionError\n\n            self.index = self.index + 1\n            if isinstance(x, ListConfig.ValueNode):\n                return x._value()\n            raise AssertionError\n\n    def __iter__(self):\n        return self._iter_ex(True)\n\n    def _iter_ex(self, resolve: bool) -> Iterator[Any]:\n        try:\n            return ListConfig.ListIterator(self, resolve)\n        except Exception:\n            raise AssertionError from None\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._content = [\n            ListConfig.ValueNode(1),\n            ListConfig.ValueNode(3),\n            ListConfig.ValueNode(torch.tensor([7.0])),\n        ]\n\n\ndef longformer_chunk(hidden_states, window_overlap=256):\n    \"\"\"convert into overlapping chunks. def shape(states):\n            \"\"\"projection\"\"\"\n            return states.view(batch_size, -1, 8, 64).transpose(1, 2)\n\n        def project(hidden_states, proj_layer, key_value_states, past_key_value):\n            \"\"\"projects hidden states correctly to key/query states\"\"\"\n            if key_value_states is None:\n                # self-attn\n                # (batch_size, n_heads, seq_length, dim_per_head)\n                hidden_states = shape(proj_layer(hidden_states))\n            elif past_key_value is None:\n                # cross-attn\n                # (batch_size, n_heads, seq_length, dim_per_head)\n                hidden_states = shape(proj_layer(key_value_states))\n\n            if past_key_value is not None:\n                if key_value_states is None:\n                    # self-attn\n                    # (batch_size, n_heads, key_length, dim_per_head)\n                    hidden_states = torch.cat([past_key_value, hidden_states], query_states = shape(\n            self.q(hidden_states)\n        )  # (batch_size, n_heads, seq_length, dim_per_head)\n\n        # get key/value states\n        key_states = project(\n            hidden_states,\n            self.k,\n            key_value_states,\n            past_key_value[0] if past_key_value is not None else None,\n        )\n        value_states = project(\n            hidden_states,\n            self.v,\n            key_value_states,\n            past_key_value[1] if past_key_value is not None else None,\n        )\n\n        # compute scores\n        scores = torch.matmul(query_states, key_states.transpose(3, 2))\n\n        # (truncated here )\n        return scores, value_states\n\n\nclass ChunkReformerFeedForward(torch.nn.Module):\n    # simplified from HF modeling_reformer.py\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        super().__init__()\n        self.layer_norm = torch.nn.LayerNorm(256, eps=1e-12)\n        self.dense = torch.nn.Linear(256, 256)\n FakeMamlInner()\n        self.update_step_test = 10\n        self.update_lr = 0.4\n\n    def forward(self, x_spt, y_spt, x_qry, y_qry):\n        querysz = x_qry.size(0)\n\n        corrects = [0 for _ in range(self.update_step_test + 1)]\n\n        # in order to not ruin the state of running_mean/variance and bn_weight/bias\n        # we finetuning on the copied model instead of self.net\n        net = deepcopy(self.net)\n\n        # 1. run the i-th task and compute loss for k=0\n        logits = net(x_spt)\n        loss = F.cross_entropy(logits, y_spt)\n        grad = torch.autograd.grad(loss, net.parameters())\n        fast_weights = [\n            p[1] - self.update_lr * p[0] for p in zip(grad, net.parameters())\n        ]\n\n        # this is the loss and accuracy before first update\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            # [setsz, nway]\n            logits_q = net(x_qry, net.parameters(), bn_training=True)\n            # [setsz]\n            pred_q = F.softmax(logits_q, dim=1).argmax(dim=1)\n            # scalar\n            correct = torch.eq(pred_q, y_qry).sum().item()\n            corrects[0] = corrects[0] + correct\n\n        # this is the loss and accuracy after the first update\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            # [setsz, nway]\n            logits_q = net(x_qry, fast_weights, bn_training=True)\n            # [setsz]\n            pred_q = F.softmax(logits_q, dim=1).argmax(dim=1)\n            # scalar\n            correct = torch.eq(pred_q, y_qry).sum().item()\n            corrects[1] = corrects[1] + correct\n\n        del net\n\n        accs = torch.tensor(corrects) / querysz\n\n        return accs\n\n\ndef softmax_backward_data(parent, grad_output, output, dim, self):\n    from torch import _softmax_backward_data\n\n    return _softmax_backward_data(grad_output, output, parent.dim, self.dtype)\n\n\nclass XSoftmax(torch.autograd.Function):\n    # transformers.models.deberta.modeling_deberta.XSoftmax\n    @staticmethod\n    def forward(self, input, mask, dim):\n        self.dim = dim\n        rmask = ~(mask.to(torch.bool))\n        output = input.masked_fill(rmask, torch.tensor(torch.finfo(input.dtype).min))\n        output = torch.softmax(output, self.dim)\n        output.masked_fill_(rmask, 0)\n        self.save_for_backward(output, rmask)\n        return output\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def backward(self, grad_output):\n        output, _ = self.saved_tensors\n        inputGrad = softmax_backward_data(self, grad_output, output, self.dim, output)\n        return inputGrad, None, None\n\n\nclass ModelOutput(collections.OrderedDict):\n    \"\"\"based on file_utils.py in HuggingFace\"\"\"\n\n    def __getitem__(self, k):\n that torch.argsort is stable.\n    # torch.argsort is not stable on its own\n    scale_offset = torch.arange(vector.shape[dim], device=vector.device).view(1, 1, -1)\n    scale_offset = scale_offset.expand(vector.shape)\n    scaled_vector = vector.shape[dim] * vector + (scale_offset % vector.shape[dim])\n    return torch.argsort(scaled_vector, dim=dim)\n\n\ndef _get_sorted_bucket_idx_and_undo_sorted_bucket_idx(buckets):\n    \"\"\"from hf_Reformer\"\"\"\n    # no gradients are needed\n    with torch.no_grad():\n        # hash-based sort\n dim_feedforward=2048,\n        dropout=0.1,\n        activation=nn.ReLU(),\n        layer_norm_eps=1e-5,\n    ):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.self_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(d_model, fails\n            return torch.sin(torch.cos(x))\n\n        def fn(x):\n            with torch.enable_grad():\n                a = torch.sin(x)\n                b = reversible(a)\n                c = torch.sigmoid(b)\n                c.sum().backward()\n                return x.grad\n\n        x = torch.randn(3, requires_grad=True)\n        x.grad = None\n        with torch.no_grad():\n False\n\n        # See https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/96488\n        @contextlib.contextmanager\n        def ctx():\n            try:\n                yield\n            except RuntimeError:\n                nonlocal hit_handler\n                hit_handler = True\n\n        @torch.compile(backend=\"eager\")\n        def f():\n            with ctx():\n                h()\n\n https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/96488\n        #\n        # NB: yes, [(...)] is intentional, this is a list containing a\n        # generator\n        generator_box = [(x for x in [1, 2, 3])]\n\n        counter = torch._dynamo.testing.CompileCounter()\n\n        def g(x):\n            return x + 2\n\n        # TODO: This test is pretty delicate.  To test if it's actually doing\n        # anything, rebuild eval_frame.c with '#define TORCHDYNAMO_DEBUG 1'\n        # and then look at the logs for:\n        #\n        # TRACE[_custom_eval_frame:650] begin <genexpr> test_repros.py 2276 -1 0 0\n        # TRACE[_custom_eval_frame:664] throw <genexpr>\n        #\n        # This means we're actually hitting the relevant codepath\n\n        # NB: Make sure we don't actually Dynamo this frame; if we do Dynamo\n        # this frame, Dynamo actually DOES understand list.clear and will\n        # arrange for the generator deallocation to happen when the eval frame\n        # handler is disabled, which will prevent the bug from happening (we\n        # specifically want to trigger the generator deallocation WHILE the\n        # dynamo eval frame handler is active), as that will cause the\n        # generator to become exhausted and trigger the throw_flag == TRUE\n        # case.\n        @torch._dynamo.disable(recursive=False)\n        def f(x):\n            generator_box.clear()\n            return g(x)\n\n        self.assertNoUnraisable(\n            lambda: torch.compile(f, backend=counter)(torch.randn(3))\n        )\n\n        # Make sure the x + 2 is captured (a previous incorrect implementation\n        # of this fix would have disabled the eval frame callback, which means\n        # g wouldn't get traced\n        self.assertEqual(counter.op_count, 1)\n\n    def test_error_return_without_exception_set(self):\n        #  def __getitem__(self, key):\n                content = super().__getitem__(key)\n                cls, kwargs = content if isinstance(content, tuple) else (content, {})\n                return test_detectron2_instances_cat(self):\n        class Instances:\n            def __init__(self, image_size: tuple[int, int], **kwargs: Any):\n                self._image_size = image_size\n                self._fields: dict[str, Any] = {}\n                for k, v in kwargs.items():\n                    self.set(k, v)\n\n            @property\n            def image_size(self) -> tuple[int, int]:\n                return self._image_size\n\n            def __setattr__(self, name: str, val: Any) -> None:\n                if name.startswith(\"_\"):\n                    super().__setattr__(name, val)\n                else:\n                    self.set(name, val)\n\n            def __getattr__(self, name: str) -> Any:\n                if name == \"_fields\" or name not in self._fields:\n                    raise AttributeError(\n                        f\"Cannot find field '{name}' in the given Instances!\"\n                    )\n                return self._fields[name]\n\n            def __len__(self) -> int:\n                for v in self._fields.values():\n                    # use __len__ because len() has to be int and is not friendly to tracing\n                    return v.__len__()\n                raise NotImplementedError(\"Empty Instances does not support __len__!\")\n\n            def set(self, name: str, value: Any) -> None:\n                with warnings.catch_warnings(record=True):\n                    data_len = len(value)\n                if len(self._fields):\n                    assert len(self) == data_len, (\n                        f\"Adding a field of length {data_len} to a Instances of length {len(self)}\"\n                    )\n                self._fields[name] = value\n\n            def get(self, name: str) -> Any:\n                return self._fields[name]\n\n            @staticmethod\n            def cat(instance_lists: list[\"Instances\"]) -> \"Instances\":\n                assert all(isinstance(i, Instances) for i in instance_lists)\n                assert len(instance_lists) > 0\n                if len(instance_lists) == 1:\n                    return instance_lists[0]\n\n                image_size = instance_lists[0].image_size\n                if not isinstance(\n                    image_size, torch.Tensor\n                ):  # could be a tensor in tracing\n                    for i in instance_lists[1:]:\n                        assert i.image_size == image_size\n                ret = Instances(image_size)\n                for k in instance_lists[0]._fields.keys():\n                    values = [i.get(k) for i in instance_lists]\n                    v0 = values[0]\n                    if isinstance(v0, torch.Tensor):\n                        values = torch.cat(values, dim=0)\n                    elif isinstance(v0, list):\n                        values = list(itertools.chain(*values))\n                    elif hasattr(type(v0), \"cat\"):\n                        values = type(v0).cat(values)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\n                            f\"Unsupported type {type(v0)} for concatenation\"\n                        )\n @skipIfWindows(msg=\"TODO: (xuhancn) fix, AssertionError: False is not true\")\n    def test_weakref_callback(self):\n        called1 = False\n\n        def callback1(ref):\n            nonlocal # https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/132200\n    def test_partitioner_cse_respects_mutation_boundaries(self):\n        set_available = hasattr(torch.ops, \"fsdp\") and hasattr(torch.ops.fsdp, \"set_\")\n        if not set_available:\n            return\n\n        @torch.compile(backend=\"aot_eager_decomp_partition\")\n        def f(x, l):\n            # z0 and z1 can be CSEd\n            z0 = x.sin()\n            z1 = x.sin()\n            y = x + 1\n            torch.ops.fsdp.copy_.default(x, y)\n            # z3 and z3 can be CSEd with each other,\n            # but *not* with z0/z1 (they cross a mutation boundary)\n            z2 = x.sin()\n            z3 = x.sin()\n            return z0, z1, z2, z3, l**2\n\n        x = torch.randn(3)\n        x_clone = x.clone()\n        l = torch.randn(3, requires_grad=True)\n        z0, z1, z2, z3, _ = f(x, l)\n\n        # the partitioner runs CSE. We expect that of the 4 sin() ops above:\n        # - the first 2 are CSE'd\n        # - the last 2 are CSE'd\n        # - the set_() op in the middle is a mutation barrier, preventing CSE\n        self.assertEqual(z0, (x_clone).sin())\n        self.assertEqual(z1, (x_clone).sin())\n        self.assertEqual(z2, (x_clone + 1).sin())\n        self.assertEqual(z3, (x_clone + 1).sin())\n\n    # https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/132197\n    def test_fsdp_set_input_mutation_applied_when_input_gets_no_gradients(self):\n        set_available = hasattr(torch.ops, \"fsdp\") and hasattr(torch.ops.fsdp, \"set_\")\n        if not set_available:\n            return\n\n        @torch.compile(backend=\"aot_eager_decomp_partition\")\n        def f(x, l):\n            z = x.sin()  # noqa: F841\n            y = x + 1\n            # graph input has its storage mutated\n            torch.ops.fsdp.copy_.default(x, y)\n            z2 = x.sin()\n            return z2, l**2\n\n        x = torch.randn(3)\n        x_test = x.clone()\n        l = torch.randn(3, requires_grad=True)\n        result, _ = f(x, l)\n        result_test, _ = torch.compile(f, backend=\"aot_eager_decomp_partition\")(\n            x_test, l\n        )\n\n        self.assertEqual(result, result_test)\n        self.assertEqual(x, x_test)\n\n    def test_aot_autograd_runtime_wrapper_prologue_profiled(self):\n        # Names for prologue profiling event\n        prologue_name = \"AOTDispatcher Runtime Wrapper Prologue\"\n\n        # Simple linear op to compile\n        mod = torch.nn.Linear(4, 4)\n        opt_mod = torch.compile(mod)\n        x = torch.randn(4, 4)\n\n        # Run this test with grad and no-grad to test both boolean cases trace_joint\n        for c in [contextlib.nullcontext, torch.no_grad]:\n            # Run compiled op with profiling\n            with c():\n                # warmup before profiling\n                opt_mod(x)\n                with profile(activities=[ProfilerActivity.CPU]) as prof:\n                    opt_mod(x)\n\n            # Make sure events are populated then find prologue event and last start time\n            events = prof.events()\n            self.assertTrue(events is not None)\n\n            prologue_event = None\n            last_start_time = 0\n            for event in events:\n                if hasattr(event, \"name\") and prologue_name in event.name:\n                    prologue_event = event\n                if event.time_range.start > last_start_time:\n                    last_start_time = event.time_range.start\n\n            # Make sure prologue event exist\n            self.assertTrue(prologue_event is not None)\n\n            # Make sure there is at least one other event (compiled function) that starts\n            # after prologue starts\n            self.assertLess(prologue_event.time_range.end, last_start_time)\n\n    def test_changing_stride(self):\n        cnt = torch._dynamo.testing.CompileCounter()\n\n        @torch.compile(backend=cnt)\n        def fn(x, y):\n            return x * y\n\n        for i in range(1, 4):\n            x = torch.randn(4, i)\n\n            # This is a case where we had an input that was marked unbacked:\n        # size=[2, u0], stride=[1, 1] which is bad. We want it to actually\n        # be size=[2, u0], stride=[u0, 1]. See more in the issue below:\n        # https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/142024\n\n        @torch.compile(backend=\"eager\", fullgraph=True)\n        def fn(aot6_sub_58, aot6_mul_170):\n            aot6_unsqueeze_14 = torch.ops.aten.unsqueeze.default(aot6_mul_170, 1)\n            return torch.ops.aten.mul.Tensor(aot6_sub_58, aot6_unsqueeze_14)\n\n        aot6_sub_58 = torch.randn(2, 1)\n        torch._dynamo.decorators.mark_unbacked(aot6_sub_58, 1)\n        aot6_mul_170 = torch.randn(2)\n\n        # No assert necessary since this used to crash.\n        fn(aot6_sub_58, aot6_mul_170)\n\n    @torch._dynamo.config.patch(guard_nn_modules=False)\n    @torch._dynamo.config.patch(inline_inbuilt_nn_modules=False)\n    def test_inlining_cornercase(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        nn.Modules can be mapped to either NNModuleVariable or UnspecializedNNModuleVariable. For NNModuleVariable, the\n        tensor attributes become part of the Dynamo graph. For unspecialized, they are lifted as inputs.\n\n        But there is a cornercase. Suppose you have NNModuleVariable with a submodule that is\n        UnspecializedNNModuleVariable. Today, Dynamo will still consider the submodule as specialized (courtesy of\n        guard.source().is_nn_module()). In retrospect, this is a mistake but there are dependencies of export and also\n        cudagraphs which make it harder to fix the corner case right away. The long term solution is\n        inline_inbuilt_nn_modules anyways, so we might have to live with this cornercase in the short term.\n\n        We are starting to annotate the source of each nn module more precisely - NNModuleVariable attribute is marked\n        as NNModuleSource, UnspecilaizedNNModuleVariable attribute is marked as UnspecializedNNModuleSource. But this\n        changes the behavior for the cornercase. And fails some tests which have unfortunately relied on this behavior.\n\n\n        To solve this, we tag the source only when inline_inbuilt_nn_module flag is turned on.\n\n        In this test, we purposely turn the flag off, testing that the tagging is disabled.\n        \"\"\"\n\n        class SubMod(torch.nn.Module):\n            def __init__(self):\n                super().__init__()\n                self.linear = torch.nn.Linear(1, 1)\n                self.a = torch.randn(1, 1)\n                self.counter = 0\n                self.multipliers = [2.2, 3.3]\n\n            def forward(self, x):\n                self.counter += 1\n                return (\n                    self.linear(x) * self.a * self.multipliers[0] * self.multipliers[1]\n                )\n\n        class Mod(torch.nn.Module):\n            def __init__(self):\n                super().__init__()\n                self.submod = SubMod()\n\n            def forward(self, x):\n                return self.submod(x)\n\n        mod = Mod()\n        opt_mod = torch.compile(mod, backend=\"eager\")\n\n        x = torch.randn(1, 1)\n        ref = mod(x)  # noqa: F841\n        res = opt_mod(x)  # noqa: F841\n\n        mod.submod.multipliers = [3.3, 4.4]\n        # Since guard_nn_modules is False, this will not recompile\n        with torch._dynamo.config.patch(error_on_recompile=True):\n            ref = mod(x)  # noqa: F841\n            res = opt_mod(x)  # noqa: F841\n\n    def test_optimized_module_training(self):\n        mod = torch.nn.Linear(3, 3)\n        mod.eval()\n\n        opt_mod = torch.compile(mod, backend=\"eager\")\n        self.assertFalse(opt_mod.training)\n\n        opt_mod.train()\n        self.assertTrue(opt_mod.training)\n        self.assertTrue(mod.training)\n\n        mod.eval()\n        self.assertFalse(opt_mod.training)\n\n    def test_optimized_module_patched_init(self):\n        # A regression test for #138157, and the pattern acame from deepspeed.\n        class MyModule(torch.nn.Module):\n            def __init__(self):\n                super().__init__()\n\n            def forward(self, x):\n                return x.mul(5.0)\n\n        def patch_init(init):\n            @functools.wraps(init)\n            def wrapper(module, *args, **kwargs):\n                if not hasattr(module, \"_ds_child_entered\"):\n                    # child's __init__ was called, since parents all see the same object they can now skip post_init\n                    module._ds_child_entered = True\n                init(module, *args, **kwargs)\n\n            return wrapper\n\n        def patch_init_for_class(cls):\n            if \"__init__\" in cls.__dict__:\n                cls._old_init = cls.__init__\n                cls.__init__ = patch_init(cls.__init__)\n\n        patch_init_for_class(MyModule)\n        mod = MyModule()\n        opt_mod = torch.compile(mod)\n\n        x = torch.rand(10)\n        ref = mod(x)\n        res = opt_mod(x)\n\n        self.assertEqual(ref, res)\n\n    def test_os_fspath(self):\n        @torch.compile(backend=\"eager\", fullgraph=True)\n        def fn(x):\n            os.fspath(\".\")\n            return torch.sin(x)\n\n        fn(torch.randn(4))\n\n    @requires_cuda\n    # *bs):\n            for b in bs:\n                a = a.unflatten(0, (b.shape[0], -1)).unflatten(-1, (b.shape[-1], -1))\n                a = a * b[:, None, :, None]\n                a = torch.clamp(amax_t.float(), min=1e-12) / max_v\n            t_fp8 = mul_tiled(t, scale_t.reciprocal()).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)\n            return t_fp8, scale_t\n\n        def matmul(first, amax_first, second_t, amax_second_t, bias):\n            first_fp8, scale_first = scale(first, amax_first)\n            second_t_fp8, scale_second_t = scale(second_t, amax_second_t)\n            post_scales = []\n            post_bias = None\n            post_scales = [scale_first, scale_second_t.t()]\n            scale_first = scale_first.new_ones((1, 1))\n            scale_second_t =     class Fp8LinearFn(torch.autograd.Function):\n            @staticmethod\n            def forward(ctx, a, b_t, bias):\n                amax_a = a.abs().unflatten(-1, (1, -1)).amax(dim=-1)\n                amax_b_t = b_t.abs().unflatten(-1, (1, -1)).amax(dim=-1)\n                out = matmul(a, amax_a, b_t, amax_b_t, bias)\n                ctx.a_requires_grad = a.requires_grad\n                ctx.b_requires_grad = b_t.requires_grad\n                ctx.bias_requires_grad = (\n                    bias.requires_grad if bias is not None else False\n                )\n                ctx.save_for_backward(a, b_t, amax_b_t)\n                return out\n\n            @staticmethod\n            def backward(ctx, grad_out):\n                a, b_t, amax_b_t = ctx.saved_tensors\n                # Workaround for https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/141881.\n                # The partitioner would pre-compute the transposed scaling of the weight\n                # in the forward (as it's most efficient, but it actually uses too much\n                # memory). We prevent that by making the scaling depend on the gradient\n                # in a way that has no effect and will be optimized away later.\n                # Care is needed to support tensor amax_b.repeat_interleave(\n                        b.shape[0] // amax_b.shape[0], dim=0, output_size=b.shape[0]\n                    )\n                    grad_a = matmul(grad_out, amax_grad_out, b, amax_b, None)\n                else:\n                    grad_a = None\n                if ctx.b_requires_grad:\n                    grad_b = grad_out.t() @ a\n                else:\n grad_a, grad_b, grad_bias\n\n        class Mod(torch.nn.Module):\n            def __init__(self):\n                super().__init__()\n                self.a = torch.nn.Parameter(\n            def __init__(self):\n                super().__init__()\n                self.ops_counter = defaultdict(int)\n\n            def __torch_dispatch__(self, func, types, args=(), kwargs=None):\n                if kwargs is None:\n                    kwargs = {}\n                rs = func(*args, **kwargs)\n                self.ops_counter[func] += 1\n                return
